* Document title Baby One More Time
* Sentence ... Baby One More Time is the debut Album by American pop icon Britney Spears .
* Sentence It was released on January 12 , 1999 through Jive Records .
* Sentence In June 1997 , while Spears negotiated with her manager at the time , Lou Pearlman , to join female pop group Innosense , her mother , Lynne Spears , asked a Spears’ family friend and entertainment lawyer , Larry Rudolph , for his opinion .
* Sentence Rudolph took interest and decided to pitch her to record labels .
* Sentence Rudolph submitted a tape of Britney Spears singing over a Whitney Houston Karaoke song , along with a demo tape of an unused song from Toni Braxton .
* Sentence Jive Records was interested and appointed the singer to work with producer Eric Foster White .
* Sentence After hearing the recorded material , Jive signed Spears to a multi - album deal .
* Sentence Spears traveled to Sweden to work with producers Max Martin , Denniz Pop , and Rami Yacoub , among others .
* Sentence Martin presented a track titled Hit Me Baby ( One More Time ) to Spears and her management , which had been rejected by girl group TLC .
* Sentence Spears later claimed that she felt excited when she heard it and knew it was going to be a hit record .
* Sentence Her debut album was completed in June 1998 , and the song was released as ... Baby One More Time as Spears ' debut single in October .
* Sentence The single became a global success , reaching number one in every country it charted in , became the best - selling song of 1999 in the UK , and has since become one of the best - selling singles of all - time , selling over 10 million copies .
* Sentence Upon release , the album received mixed reviews from music critics , with many labeling it silly and premature .
* Sentence ... Baby One More Time was a large commercial success , debuting atop the Billboard 200 chart and Canadian Albums Chart , and reached the top 5 in several countries .
* Sentence It also received worldwide certifications , including a 14× platinum ( diamond ) certification from the Recording Industry Association of America ( RIAA ) , for shipments of over 14 million copies in the US .
* Sentence ... Baby One More Time is Spears ' most successful album with sales of 32 million copies worldwide , making it one of the best - selling albums of all - time and the best - selling album by a teenage solo artist .
* Sentence Four additional singles were released from the album and Spears heavily promoted it through interviews and performances on national television .
* Sentence She embarked on the ... Baby One More Time Tour in 1999 , and later continued on a second leg title the Crazy 2k Tour .
* Sentence ... Baby One More Time earned Spears Grammy Award nominations for Best New Artist and Best Female Pop Vocal Performance for ... Baby One More Time at the 42nd Annual Grammy Awards in 2000 .

* Sentence Background and development ;
* Sentence In June 1997 , Spears was in talks with manager Lou Pearlman to join female pop group Innosense .
* Sentence Lynne asked family friend and entertainment lawyer Larry Rudolph for his opinion and submitted a tape of Spears singing over a Whitney Houston karaoke song along with some pictures .
* Sentence Rudolph decided to pitch her to record labels , which required a professional demo .
* Sentence He sent Spears an unused song from Toni Braxton ;
* Sentence she rehearsed for a week and recorded in a studio with a sound engineer .
* Sentence Spears traveled to New York with the demo and met executives from four labels , returning to Kentwood the same day .
* Sentence Three rejected her , arguing audiences wanted pop bands such as the Backstreet Boys and the Spice Girls , and there was n't going to be another Madonna , another Debbie Gibson or another Tiffany .
* Sentence Two weeks later , executives from Jive Records returned calls to Rudolph .
* Sentence Senior vice president of A&R Jeff Fenster stated , It 's very rare to hear someone that age who can deliver emotional content and commercial appeal .
* Sentence [ ... ] For any artist , the motivation — the ' eye of the tiger'— is extremely important .
* Sentence And Britney had that .
* Sentence They appointed her to work with producer Eric Foster White for a month , who reportedly shaped her voice from lower and less poppy delivery to distinctively , unmistakably Britney .
* Sentence Spears recorded ten songs with White , including Autumn Goodbye , E - Mail My Heart , From the Bottom of My Broken Heart , I 'm So Curious , I Will Still Love You , Luv The Hurt Away , Soda Pop , Thinkin ' About You , and You Got It All .
* Sentence The singer also recorded a cover of Sonny & Cher 's 1967 single The Beat Goes On .
* Sentence White was responsible for the vocal recording and song production , while additional production was done by English electronic music group All Seeing I .
* Sentence After hearing the material , president Clive Calder ordered a full album .
* Sentence Spears flew to Cheiron Studios in Stockholm , Sweden , where half of the album was recorded from March to April 1998 , with producers Max Martin , Denniz Pop and Rami Yacoub , among others .
* Sentence Martin showed Spears and her management a track titled Hit Me Baby One More Time , which was originally written for American Rhythm and blues group TLC ;
* Sentence however , they rejected it .
* Sentence Spears later claimed that she felt excited when she heard it and knew it was going to be a hit .
* Sentence We at Jive said , ' This is a fuckin ' smash ' , revealed the label 's A&R executive , Steven Lunt ;
* Sentence however , other executives were concerned that the line Hit Me would condone Domestic violence , and later revised it to ... Baby One More Time .
* Sentence The singer revealed that she did n't do well at all the first day in the studio [ recording the song ] , I was just too nervous .
* Sentence So I went out that night and had some fun .
* Sentence The next day I was completely relaxed and nailed it .
* Sentence You got ta be relaxed singing ' ... Baby One More Time ' .
* Sentence By June 1998 , the album was done , and Spears embarked on a promotional tour sponsored by L'Oréal .
* Sentence ... Baby One More Time was released as Spears ' debut album on January 12 , 1999 .

* Sentence Music and lyrics ;
* Sentence Spears originally envisioned Sheryl Crow music , but younger more adult contemporary , but felt all right with her label 's producers , since It made more sense to go pop , because I can dance to it — it 's more me .
* Sentence The album opens with the first single ... Baby One More Time , a Teen pop and Dance - pop song that begins with a three - note motif in the bass range of the Piano .
* Sentence The opening was compared to many other songs , such as We Will Rock You ( 1977 ) , Start Me Up ( 1981 ) , These Words ( 2004 ) and the theme song of the film Jaws due to the fact the track makes its presence known in exactly one second .
* Sentence According to magazine Blender , ... Baby One More Time is composed by wah - wah guitar lines and EKG -machine bass - slaps .
* Sentence Claudia Mitchell and Jacqueline Reid - Walsh , authors of Girl Culture :
* Sentence Studying girl culture :
* Sentence a readers ' guide ( 2008 ) , observed that the lyrics of the song gesture toward [ Spears ] longing for the return of an ex - boyfriend .
* Sentence The next song and third single , ( You Drive Me ) Crazy runs through a moderately slow dance beat , and has a rhythm and blues Melody mixed with edgy synthesized instrumentals .
* Sentence The third track and second single Sometimes is a ballad , that Spears begins with You tell me you 're in love with me / That you ca n't take your pretty eyes away from me / It 's not that I do n't wanna stay / But every time you come too close I move away .
* Sentence Stephen Thomas Erlewine of AllMusic noted the song has a catchy hook and endearing melody , with a reminiscent euro - dance rhythm .
* Sentence ;
* Sentence After Sometimes is ... Baby One More Time 's fourth track , Soda Pop , a song that draws influences from Bubblegum pop and Dancehall , and features background vocals from co - writer Mikey Bassie .
* Sentence Spears ' vocals on the fifth track and fourth single , Born to Make You Happy , span more than an Octave .
* Sentence Its lyrics allude to a relationship that a woman desires to repair , not quite understanding what went wrong , as she comes to realize that I do n't know how to live without your love / I was born to make you happy .
* Sentence The sixth track and final single , From the Bottom of My Broken Heart , is a sentimental slow - tempo Teen pop ballad .
* Sentence ;
* Sentence I Will Be There is a Pop rock song that features a guitar riff similar to Natalie Imbruglia 's Torn ( 1997 ) , with a rousing chorus about standing by your man ( or a best friend or a house pet ) , as noted by Kyle Anderson of MTV .
* Sentence The eleventh track , E - Mail My Heart , is a sensitive piano ballad where Spears sings , E - mail me back/ And say our love will stay alive .
* Sentence The cover of Sonny & Cher 's 1967 single The Beat Goes On is influenced by Bossa nova and Trip hop , and features a similar sound to spy movies themes .

* Sentence ... Baby One More Time was released in North America and Philippines on January 12 , 1999 , in Japan on February 24 and in Europe and Oceania on March 8 .
* Sentence The album was re - released in Europe on June 30 , 2003 , and the digital deluxe edition was released on December 25 , 2007 ( Christmas ) in the United States .
* Sentence On August 14 , 2017 , it was announced that 2,500 pink and white swirled copies of ... Baby One More Time would be released on vinyl exclusively through Urban Outfitters on November 3 , 2017 ;
* Sentence the vinyl was made available for pre - order that day .
* Sentence Promotion began in 1998 , when Spears did a small tour in malls and food courts that were located mostly in larger cities around the United States and Canada .
* Sentence Each show lasted around thirty minutes , and Spears had two male dancers with her on the stage .
* Sentence The promo tour is also known as the L'Oréal Mall Tour , after its sponsor .
* Sentence The singer made several promotional appearances including talk shows and live performances around the world .
* Sentence In December 1998 , Spears ' first showed up on MTV 's and the Box 's most - requested video charts .
* Sentence She also appeared on the Ricki Lake Show , the Howie Mandel Show , and was the presenter of the 1999 American Music Awards , prior to the release of the album .
* Sentence The singer also appeared on MTV 's Spring break and on the hundredth episode of Nickelodeon 's All That .
* Sentence However , after hurting her knee , she had rescheduled appearances several shows such as The Tonight Show with Jay Leno and Live with Regis and Kathie Lee .
* Sentence After recovering , Spears embarked on another promotional schedule .
* Sentence The singer appeared on 12th Annual Nickelodeon s Kids ' Choice Awards on May 1 , MTV 's FANatic on May 12 , Live with Regis and Kathie Lee on May 3 , and The Rosie O'Donnell Show on May 25 .

* Sentence The episode aired on September 24 , 1999 .
* Sentence The same month , Spears performed on The Rosie O'Donnell Show on September 27 , and visited Carson Daly on MTV 's Total Request Live the following day .

* Sentence Singles ;
* Sentence ... Baby One More Time was released as Spears ' debut single on October 23 , 1998 .
* Sentence The song received generally favorable critical reviews , mostly praising its composition .
* Sentence ... Baby One More Time attained worldwide success , reaching number one in every European country where it charted .
* Sentence It received numerous certifications around the world , and is one of the best - selling singles of all time , at over ten million copies .
* Sentence An accompanying music video , directed by Nigel Dick , portrays Spears as a student from a Catholic high school , who starts to Daydream that she is singing and dancing around the school , while watching her love interest from afar .
* Sentence In 2010 , the music video for ... Baby One More Time was voted the third - most influential video in the history of Pop music .
* Sentence ;
* Sentence Sometimes was released as the second single on April 30 , 1999 .
* Sentence Sometimes achieved commercial success worldwide , reaching number one on Ultratop Flanders Singles in Belgium , Single Top 100 in Netherlands and RIANZ Singles in New Zealand , while peaking inside the top five in four countries .
* Sentence In the United States , Sometimes missed the top - twenty , peaking at number twenty - one on the Billboard Hot 100 .
* Sentence The music video for the song was directed by Nigel Dick .
* Sentence During rehearsals , on February 11 , 1999 , Spears injured her left knee and needed surgery .
* Sentence After recuperating in Kentwood , Louisiana , the music video was shot on April 9–10 , 1999 at Paradise Cove in Malibu , California .
* Sentence ;
* Sentence It was released on May 6 , 1999 , on MTV 's Total Request Live .
* Sentence In May 1999 , Max Martin and Spears went to the Battery Studios in New York City , to re - record the vocals of ( You Drive Me ) Crazy , for a reproduced version called The Stop ! Remix that was going to be included on the original motion picture soundtrack of the film Drive Me Crazy ( 1999 ) .
* Sentence The Stop ! Remix of the song was released as the album 's third single on August 23 , 1999 .

* Sentence On March 5 , 1999 , it was reported that Spears was planning her first headlining tour .
* Sentence She announced that the tour would start in July .
* Sentence On May 12 , Tommy Hilfiger was announced as the main tour sponsor .
* Sentence During the time of the announcement , Spears was being featured in the company 's AllStars campaign .
* Sentence On December 17 , during the premiere of the music video of From the Bottom of My Broken Heart on TRL , Spears called the show to announce March 2000 United States tour dates .
* Sentence The extension , entitled Crazy 2k Tour , was considered a prelude to her future world tour , Oops ! ... I Did It Again Tour .
* Sentence The leg 's main sponsor was Got Milk ? .
* Sentence Media director Peter Gardiner explained , Britney is magic with teen - age girls , and that 's an absolutely crucial target for milk .
* Sentence Spears shot an advertising campaign to be shown before her performances began .
* Sentence The secondary sponsor was Polaroid and the corporation released the Polaroid i - Zone as the tour 's official camera .
* Sentence Spears used the I - Zone onstage to take pictures of the audience and further promote the product .
* Sentence The show was divided into segments , separated by interlude , ending with an encore .
* Sentence The set list consisted of songs from her debut album and several covers .
* Sentence Some changes were made during the 2000 leg , with the covers replaced by songs from her second studio album , Oops ! ... I Did It Again .
* Sentence The tour received positive critical appreciation .
* Sentence During the tour , Spears was accused of lip synching , although she denied these claims .
* Sentence On April 20 , 2000 , the concert at Hilton Hawaiian Village in Honolulu , Hawaii , was taped .
* Sentence It was slightly altered from its Crazy 2k incarnation and featured different costumes .
* Sentence On June 5 , 2000 , it was broadcast on Fox .
* Sentence The special was aired several times during the year .
* Sentence On November 21 , 2000 , JIVE Records released the Britney Spears :
* Sentence Live and More ! DVD , which included the Fox special .
* Sentence It was certified triple Platinum by the RIAA for shipping 300,000 units .

* Sentence ... Baby One More Time received mixed reviews from critics .
* Sentence Stephen Thomas Erlewine of Allmusic gave the album four out of five stars , Billboard s Paul Verna considered the album a top 40-ready workout filled with hook - laden songs from the same bag as the title cut .
* Sentence ;
* Sentence Kyle Anderson of MTV said he was surprised in more ways than one with his first listening of ... Baby One More Time , commenting he expected there to be a lot of filler ( there sort of is ) , though I did n't expect it to be as odd ( at least sonically ) as it ended up being .
* Sentence There has never been any mystery to why Spears became such a superstar , but these songs probably would have been huge even if Britney wore burlap sacks in all of her videos .
* Sentence Barry Walters of Rolling Stone gave the album two stars out of five , and compared the album 's sound to early hits of Debbie Gibson , Mariah Carey , and Samantha Fox .
* Sentence Walters also said that while several Cherion - crafted kiddie - funk jams serve up beefy hooks , shameless schlock slowies , like ' E - Mail My Heart ' , are pure spam .
* Sentence A NME reviewer rated ... Baby One More Time 1 out of 10 , saying that we seem to have reached crisis point :
* Sentence pubescent pop is now so rife that 17-year - old Britney ' lizard - lounge ' Spears is already halfway through her lucrative showbiz career .
* Sentence He also found the album premature , commenting , hopefully , if she starts to live the wretched life that we all eventually do , her voice will show the scars , she 'll stop looking so fucking smug , she 'll find solace in drugs and we 'll be all the more happier for it .
* Sentence Now grow up , girl .
* Sentence Quick ! Amanda Murray of Sputnikmusic felt that , with the exception of the terrific title track , ... Baby One More Time is a collection of either competent pop songs underwhelmingly executed or underwhelmingly written pop songs competently executed .

* Sentence ... Baby One More Time debuted at number one on the Billboard 200 selling 121,000 units , replacing DMX 's Flesh of My Flesh , Blood of My Blood ( 1998 ) .
* Sentence Spears broke several records by doing so .
* Sentence The singer became the first new female artist to have a number one single on the Billboard Hot 100 and number one album on the Billboard 200 at the same time ;
* Sentence the first new artist ( male or female ) to have a single go to the number one spot the same week that the album debuted at number one ;
* Sentence and the first new female artist to have the first single and first album at number one the same week .
* Sentence Spears is also the youngest female in Billboard history to have a simultaneous single and album at number one in the same week .
* Sentence After four weeks since its release , the album had sold more than 500,000 copies , according to Nielsen SoundScan sales data .
* Sentence After dropping to the top five , the album went back to number one in its fourth week , with a total of 804,200 units sold .
* Sentence On its fifth week it reached its highest sales week with 229,000 copies sold .
* Sentence ... Baby One More Time spent a total of six non - consecutive weeks at number one , and sold more than 1.8 million copies in its first two months of release in the country .
* Sentence In its forty - seventh week on the Billboard 200 , the album held strong at number three , and with sales of over of 10 million copies in the United States alone .
* Sentence The album was later certified diamond by the Recording Industry Association of America ( RIAA ) , making Spears the youngest artist to receive that award , breaking Alanis Morissette 's record , who was 21 years old when she released Jagged Little Pill ( 1995 ) .
* Sentence The album was the 14th album since 1991 to sell over 10 million copies in the United States , and Spears became the best - selling female artist of 1999 .
* Sentence ... Baby One More Time spent a total of 51 weeks in the top 10 of the Billboard 200 .
* Sentence The album spent a total of one - hundred - and - three weeks on the chart .
* Sentence ... Baby One More Time landed at number three on Bertelsmann Music Group all - time best - sellers list , selling 1.6 million units , behind Shania Twain 's Come on Over ( 1997 ) .
* Sentence ;
* Sentence The album debuted at number one on the Canadian Albums Chart , totaling nine non - consecutive weeks at the top .
* Sentence On December 12 , 1999 , the Music Canada ( CRIA ) certified it diamond , for sales over one million units .
* Sentence ... Baby One More Time spent two weeks at number two on the European Top 100 Albums , and sold over four million copies within the continent , being certified quadruple platinum by the International Federation of the Phonographic Industry ( IFPI ) .
* Sentence The album reached number two on the UK Albums Chart , number four on French Albums Chart and was certified triple platinum by the British Phonographic Industry ( BPI ) , double platinum by the Syndicat National de l'Édition Phonographique ( SNEP ) , triple gold in Germany by the International Federation of the Phonographic Industry ( IFPI ) , and decuple platinum ( diamond ) by the Polish Society of the Phonographic Industry ( ZPAV ) .
* Sentence ... Baby One More Time debuted at number nine in May 1999 on the ARIA Albums Chart in Australia , reaching number two nine weeks later , placing behind the Dawson 's Creek soundtrack .
* Sentence The album became the seventh highest - selling of 1999 in the country , and was certified quadruple platinum by the Australian Recording Industry Association ( ARIA ) the following year after shipping 280,000 copies to retailers .
* Sentence The album debuted at number three on the RIANZ Albums Chart in New Zealand , placing behind Shania Twain 's Come on Over ( 1997 ) and The Corrs ' Talk on Corners ( 1997 ) .
* Sentence The album was later certified triple platinum in the country by the Recorded Music NZ ( RIANZ ) .
